#### Lisa (OCaml FFI & C++):
1. **Ctypes.Structured vs Marshaling**:
   - Use **Ctypes.Structured** for better integration and memory management when dealing with structured data.
   - Manual marshaling can lead to inconsistencies with large arrays.

2. **Memory Leaks**:
   - Rely on **manual finalizers** for C++ objects to improve garbage collection reliability over `Gc.finalise`.
   - Implement explicit destructors for complex objects managed across bindings.

3. **Debugging Segfaults**:
